40   override def transform(ref: SingleDenotation)(implicit ctx: Context): SingleDenotation = ref

50   override def transformMatch(tree: Match)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
51     val translated = new Translator()(ctx).translator.translateMatch(tree)
52 
53     // check exhaustivity and unreachability
54     val engine = new SpaceEngine
55     if (engine.checkable(tree)) {
56       engine.checkExhaustivity(tree)
57       engine.checkRedundancy(tree)
58     }
59 
60     translated.ensureConforms(tree.tpe)
61   }
62

71   trait CodegenCore {
72 
73     // assert(owner ne null); assert(owner ne NoSymbol)
74     def freshSym(pos: Position, tp: Type = NoType, unique: UniqueNameKind = PatMatStdBinderName, owner: Symbol = ctx.owner) = {
75       ctx.newSymbol(owner, unique.fresh(), Flags.Synthetic | Flags.Case, tp, coord = pos)
76     }
77 
78     def newSynthCaseLabel(unique: UniqueNameKind, tpe: Type, owner: Symbol = ctx.owner) =
79       ctx.newSymbol(owner, unique.fresh(), Flags.Label | Flags.Synthetic | Flags.Method, tpe).asTerm
80       //NoSymbol.newLabel(freshName(name), NoPosition) setFlag treeInfo.SYNTH_CASE_FLAGS
81 
82     // codegen relevant to the structure of the translation (how extractors are combined)
83     trait AbsCodegen {
84       def matcher(scrut: Tree, scrutSym: Symbol, restpe: Type)(cases: List[Casegen => Tree], matchFailGen: Option[Symbol => Tree]): Tree
85 
86       // local / context-free
87 
88       /* cast b to tp */
89       def _asInstanceOf(b: Symbol, tp: Type): Tree
90       /* a check `checker` == binder */
91       def _equals(checker: Tree, binder: Symbol): Tree
92       /* b.isIsInstanceOf[tp] */
93       def _isInstanceOf(b: Symbol, tp: Type): Tree
94       /* tgt is expected to be a Seq, call tgt.drop(n) */
95       def drop(tgt: Tree)(n: Int): Tree
96       /* tgt is expected to have method apply(int), call tgt.apply(i) */
97       def index(tgt: Tree)(i: Int): Tree
98       /* make tree that accesses the i'th component of the tuple referenced by binder */
99       def tupleSel(binder: Symbol)(i: Int): Tree
100     }
101 
102     // structure
103     trait Casegen extends AbsCodegen {
104       def one(res: Tree): Tree
105 
106       def flatMap(prev: Tree, b: Symbol, next: Tree): Tree
107       def flatMapCond(cond: Tree, res: Tree, nextBinder: Symbol, next: Tree): Tree
108       def flatMapGuard(cond: Tree, next: Tree): Tree
109       def ifThenElseZero(c: Tree, thenp: Tree): Tree =
110         If(c, thenp, zero)
111       protected def zero: Tree
112     }
113 
114     def codegen: AbsCodegen
115 
116     abstract class CommonCodegen extends AbsCodegen {
117       def tupleSel(binder: Symbol)(i: Int): Tree = ref(binder).select(nme.productAccessorName(i))
118       def index(tgt: Tree)(i: Int): Tree         = {
119         if (i > 0) tgt.select(defn.Seq_apply).appliedTo(Literal(Constant(i)))
120         else tgt.select(defn.Seq_head).ensureApplied
121       }
122 
123       // Right now this blindly calls drop on the result of the unapplySeq
124       // unless it verifiably has no drop method (this is the case in particular
125       // with Array.) You should not actually have to write a method called drop
126       // for name-based matching, but this was an expedient route for the basics.
127       def drop(tgt: Tree)(n: Int): Tree = {
128         def callDirect   = tgt.select(nme.drop).appliedTo(Literal(Constant(n)))
129         def callRuntime  = ref(defn.ScalaRuntime_drop).appliedTo(tgt, Literal(Constant(n)))
130 
131         def needsRuntime = !(tgt.tpe derivesFrom defn.SeqClass) /*typeOfMemberNamedDrop(tgt.tpe) == NoType*/
132 
133         if (needsRuntime) callRuntime else callDirect
134       }
135 
136       // NOTE: checker must be the target of the ==, that's the patmat semantics for ya
137       def _equals(checker: Tree, binder: Symbol): Tree =
138         tpd.applyOverloaded(checker, nme.EQ, List(ref(binder)), List.empty, defn.BooleanType)
139 
140       // the force is needed mainly to deal with the GADT typing hack (we can't detect it otherwise as tp nor pt need contain an abstract type, we're just casting wildly)
141       def _asInstanceOf(b: Symbol, tp: Type): Tree = ref(b).ensureConforms(tp) // andType here breaks t1048
142       def _isInstanceOf(b: Symbol, tp: Type): Tree = ref(b).select(defn.Any_isInstanceOf).appliedToType(tp)
143     }
144   }
145 
146   object Rebindings {
147     def apply(from: Symbol, to: Symbol) = new Rebindings(List(from), List(ref(to)))
148     // requires sameLength(from, to)
149     def apply(from: List[Symbol], to: List[Tree]) =
150       if (from nonEmpty) new Rebindings(from, to) else NoRebindings
151   }
152 
153   class Rebindings(val lhs: List[Symbol], val rhs: List[Tree]) {
154     def >>(other: Rebindings) = {
155       if (other eq NoRebindings) this
156       else if (this eq NoRebindings) other
157       else {
158         assert((lhs.toSet ++ other.lhs.toSet).size == lhs.length + other.lhs.length, "no double assignments")
159         new Rebindings(this.lhs ++ other.lhs, this.rhs ++ other.rhs)
160       }
161     }
162 
163     def emitValDefs: List[ValDef] = {
164       (lhs, rhs).zipped.map((symbol, tree) => ValDef(symbol.asTerm, tree.ensureConforms(symbol.info)))
165     }
166   }
167   object NoRebindings extends Rebindings(Nil, Nil)
168 
169   trait OptimizedCodegen extends CodegenCore {
170     override def codegen: AbsCodegen = optimizedCodegen
171 
172     // when we know we're targetting Option, do some inlining the optimizer won't do
173     // for example, `o.flatMap(f)` becomes `if (o == None) None else f(o.get)`, similarly for orElse and guard
174     //   this is a special instance of the advanced inlining optimization that takes a method call on
175     //   an object of a type that only has two concrete subclasses, and inlines both bodies, guarded by an if to distinguish the two cases
176     object optimizedCodegen extends CommonCodegen {
177 
178       /** Inline runOrElse and get rid of Option allocations
179         *
180         * runOrElse(scrut: scrutTp)(matcher): resTp = matcher(scrut) getOrElse ${catchAll(`scrut`)}
181         * the matcher's optional result is encoded as a flag, keepGoing, where keepGoing == true encodes result.isEmpty,
182         * if keepGoing is false, the result Some(x) of the naive translation is encoded as matchRes == x
183         */
184       def matcher(scrut: Tree, scrutSym: Symbol, restpe: Type)(cases: List[Casegen => Tree], matchFailGen: Option[Symbol => Tree]): Tree = {
185         //val matchRes = ctx.newSymbol(NoSymbol, ctx.freshName("matchRes").toTermName, Flags.Synthetic | Flags.Param | Flags.Label | Flags.Method, restpe /*withoutAnnotations*/)
186           //NoSymbol.newValueParameter(newTermName("x"), NoPosition, newFlags = SYNTHETIC) setInfo restpe.withoutAnnotations
187 
188 
189         val caseSyms: List[TermSymbol] = cases.scanLeft(ctx.owner.asTerm)((curOwner, nextTree) =>
190           newSynthCaseLabel(PatMatCaseName, MethodType(Nil, restpe), curOwner)).tail
191 
192         // must compute catchAll after caseLabels (side-effects nextCase)
193         // catchAll.isEmpty iff no synthetic default case needed (the (last) user-defined case is a default)
194         // if the last user-defined case is a default, it will never jump to the next case; it will go immediately to matchEnd
195         val catchAllDef = matchFailGen.map { _(scrutSym) }
196           .getOrElse(Throw(New(defn.MatchErrorType, List(ref(scrutSym)))))
197 
198         val matchFail = newSynthCaseLabel(PatMatMatchFailName, MethodType(Nil, restpe))
199         val catchAllDefBody = DefDef(matchFail, catchAllDef)
200 
201         val nextCases = (caseSyms.tail ::: List(matchFail)).map(ref(_).ensureApplied)
202         val caseDefs = (cases zip caseSyms zip nextCases).foldRight[Tree](catchAllDefBody) {
203           // dotty deviation
204           //case (((mkCase, sym), nextCase), acc) =>
205           (x: (((Casegen => Tree), TermSymbol), Tree), acc: Tree) => x match {
206             case ((mkCase, sym), nextCase) =>
207               val body = mkCase(new OptimizedCasegen(nextCase)).ensureConforms(restpe)
208 
209               DefDef(sym, _ => Block(List(acc), body))
210           }
211         }
212 
213         // scrutSym == NoSymbol when generating an alternatives matcher
214         // val scrutDef = scrutSym.fold(List[Tree]())(ValDef(_, scrut) :: Nil) // for alternatives
215 
216         Block(List(caseDefs), ref(caseSyms.head).ensureApplied)
217       }
218 
219       class OptimizedCasegen(nextCase: Tree) extends CommonCodegen with Casegen {
220         def matcher(scrut: Tree, scrutSym: Symbol, restpe: Type)(cases: List[Casegen => Tree], matchFailGen: Option[Symbol => Tree]): Tree =
221           optimizedCodegen.matcher(scrut, scrutSym, restpe)(cases, matchFailGen)
222 
223         // only used to wrap the RHS of a body
224         // res: T
225         // returns MatchMonad[T]
226         def one(res: Tree): Tree = /*ref(matchEnd) appliedTo*/ res // a jump to a case label is special-cased in typedApply
227         protected def zero: Tree = nextCase
228 
229         // prev: MatchMonad[T]
230         // b: T
231         // next: MatchMonad[U]
232         // returns MatchMonad[U]
233         def flatMap(prev: Tree, b: Symbol, next: Tree): Tree = {
234           val resultArity = productArity(b.info)
235           if (isProductMatch(prev.tpe, resultArity)) {
236             val nullCheck: Tree = prev.select(defn.Object_ne).appliedTo(Literal(Constant(null)))
237             ifThenElseZero(
238               nullCheck,
239               Block(
240                 List(ValDef(b.asTerm, prev)),
241                 next //Substitution(b, ref(prevSym))(next)
242               )
243             )
244           }
245           else {
246             val getDenot = extractorMember(prev.tpe, nme.get)
247             val isEmptyDenot = extractorMember(prev.tpe, nme.isEmpty)
248             assert(getDenot.exists && isEmptyDenot.exists, i"${prev.tpe}")
249 
250             val tmpSym = freshSym(prev.pos, prev.tpe, PatMatOName)
251             val prevValue = ref(tmpSym).select(getDenot.symbol).ensureApplied
252 
253             Block(
254               List(ValDef(tmpSym, prev)),
255               // must be isEmpty and get as we don't control the target of the call (prev is an extractor call)
256               ifThenElseZero(
257                 ref(tmpSym).select(isEmptyDenot.symbol).select(defn.Boolean_!),
258                 Block(List(ValDef(b.asTerm, prevValue)), next)
259               )
260             )
261           }
262         }
263 
264         // cond: Boolean
265         // res: T
266         // nextBinder: T
267         // next == MatchMonad[U]
268         // returns MatchMonad[U]
269         def flatMapCond(cond: Tree, res: Tree, nextBinder: Symbol, next: Tree): Tree = {
270           val rest = Block(List(ValDef(nextBinder.asTerm, res)), next)
271           ifThenElseZero(cond, rest)
272         }
273 
274         // guardTree: Boolean
275         // next: MatchMonad[T]
276         // returns MatchMonad[T]
277         def flatMapGuard(guardTree: Tree, next: Tree): Tree =
278           ifThenElseZero(guardTree, next)
279 
280         def flatMapCondStored(cond: Tree, condSym: Symbol, res: Tree, nextBinder: Symbol, next: Tree): Tree =
281           ifThenElseZero(cond, Block(
282             List(Assign(ref(condSym), Literal(Constant(true))),
283               Assign(ref(nextBinder), res)),
284             next
285           ))
286       }
287     }
288   }

297   trait TreeMakers extends CodegenCore {
298     def optimizeCases(prevBinder: Symbol, cases: List[List[TreeMaker]], pt: Type): (List[List[TreeMaker]], List[Tree])
299     def analyzeCases(prevBinder: Symbol, cases: List[List[TreeMaker]], pt: Type, suppression: Suppression): Unit = {}
300 
301     def emitSwitch(scrut: Tree, scrutSym: Symbol, cases: List[List[TreeMaker]], pt: Type, matchFailGenOverride: Option[Symbol => Tree], unchecked: Boolean): Option[Tree] = {
302       // TODO Deal with guards?
303 
304       def isSwitchableType(tpe: Type): Boolean =
305         (tpe isRef defn.IntClass) ||
306         (tpe isRef defn.ByteClass) ||
307         (tpe isRef defn.ShortClass) ||
308         (tpe isRef defn.CharClass)
309 
310       object IntEqualityTestTreeMaker {
311         def unapply(treeMaker: EqualityTestTreeMaker): Option[Int] = treeMaker match {
312           case EqualityTestTreeMaker(`scrutSym`, _, Literal(const), _) =>
313             if (const.isIntRange) Some(const.intValue)
314             else None
315           case _ =>
316             None
317         }
318       }
319 
320       def isSwitchCase(treeMakers: List[TreeMaker]): Boolean = treeMakers match {
321         // case 5 =>
322         case List(IntEqualityTestTreeMaker(_), _: BodyTreeMaker) =>
323           true
324 
325         // case 5 | 6 =>
326         case List(AlternativesTreeMaker(`scrutSym`, alts, _), _: BodyTreeMaker) =>
327           alts.forall {
328             case List(IntEqualityTestTreeMaker(_)) => true
329             case _ => false
330           }
331 
332         // case _ =>
333         case List(_: BodyTreeMaker) =>
334           true
335 
336         /* case x @ pat =>
337          * This includes:
338          *   case x =>
339          *   case x @ 5 =>
340          *   case x @ (5 | 6) =>
341          */
342         case (_: SubstOnlyTreeMaker) :: rest =>
343           isSwitchCase(rest)
344 
345         case _ =>
346           false
347       }
348 
349       /* (Nil, body) means that `body` is the default case
350        * It's a bit hacky but it simplifies manipulations.
351        */
352       def extractSwitchCase(treeMakers: List[TreeMaker]): (List[Int], BodyTreeMaker) = (treeMakers: @unchecked) match {
353         // case 5 =>
354         case List(IntEqualityTestTreeMaker(intValue), body: BodyTreeMaker) =>
355           (List(intValue), body)
356 
357         // case 5 | 6 =>
358         case List(AlternativesTreeMaker(_, alts, _), body: BodyTreeMaker) =>
359           val intValues = alts.map { alt =>
360             (alt: @unchecked) match {
361               case List(IntEqualityTestTreeMaker(intValue)) => intValue
362             }
363           }
364           (intValues, body)
365 
366         // case _ =>
367         case List(body: BodyTreeMaker) =>
368           (Nil, body)
369 
370         // case x @ pat =>
371         case (_: SubstOnlyTreeMaker) :: rest =>
372           /* Rebindings have been propagated, so the eventual body in `rest`
373            * contains all the necessary information. The substitution can be
374            * dropped at this point.
375            */
376           extractSwitchCase(rest)
377       }
378 
379       def doOverlap(a: List[Int], b: List[Int]): Boolean =
380         a.exists(b.contains _)
381 
382       def makeSwitch(valuesToCases: List[(List[Int], BodyTreeMaker)]): Tree = {
383         def genBody(body: BodyTreeMaker): Tree = {
384           val valDefs = body.rebindings.emitValDefs
385           if (valDefs.isEmpty) body.body
386           else Block(valDefs, body.body)
387         }
388 
389         val intScrut =
390           if (pt isRef defn.IntClass) ref(scrutSym)
391           else Select(ref(scrutSym), nme.toInt)
392 
393         val (normalCases, defaultCaseAndRest) = valuesToCases.span(_._1.nonEmpty)
394 
395         val newCases = for {
396           (values, body) <- normalCases
397         } yield {
398           val literals = values.map(v => Literal(Constant(v)))
399           val pat =
400             if (literals.size == 1) literals.head
401             else Alternative(literals)
402           CaseDef(pat, EmptyTree, genBody(body))
403         }
404 
405         val catchAllDef = {
406           if (defaultCaseAndRest.isEmpty) {
407             matchFailGenOverride.fold[Tree](
408                 Throw(New(defn.MatchErrorType, List(ref(scrutSym)))))(
409                 _(scrutSym))
410           } else {
411             /* After the default case, assuming the IR even allows anything,
412              * things are unreachable anyway and can be removed.
413              */
414             genBody(defaultCaseAndRest.head._2)
415           }
416         }
417         val defaultCase = CaseDef(Underscore(defn.IntType), EmptyTree, catchAllDef)
418 
419         Match(intScrut, newCases :+ defaultCase)
420       }
421 
422       val dealiased = scrut.tpe.widenDealias
423       if (isSwitchableType(dealiased) && cases.forall(isSwitchCase)) {
424         val valuesToCases = cases.map(extractSwitchCase)
425         val values = valuesToCases.map(_._1)
426         if (values.tails.exists { tail => tail.nonEmpty && tail.tail.exists(doOverlap(_, tail.head)) }) {
427           // TODO Deal with overlapping cases (mostly useless without guards)
428           None
429         } else {
430           Some(makeSwitch(valuesToCases))
431         }
432       } else {
433         if (dealiased hasAnnotation defn.SwitchAnnot)
434           ctx.warning("failed to emit switch for `@switch` annotated match", scrut.pos)
435         None
436       }
437     }
438 
439     // for catch (no need to customize match failure)
440     def emitTypeSwitch(bindersAndCases: List[(Symbol, List[TreeMaker])], pt: Type): Option[List[CaseDef]] =
441       None // todo

443     abstract class TreeMaker {
444       def pos: Position
445 
446       private[this] var currSub: Rebindings = null
447 
448       /** captures the scope and the value of the bindings in patterns
449         * important *when* the substitution happens (can't accumulate and do at once after the full matcher has been constructed)
450         */
451       def rebindings: Rebindings =
452         if (currSub eq null) introducedRebindings
453         else currSub
454 
455       protected def introducedRebindings: Rebindings
456 
457       private[TreeMakers] def incorporateOuterRebinding(outerSubst: Rebindings): Unit = {
458         if (currSub ne null) {
459           ctx.debuglog("BUG: incorporateOuterRebinding called more than once for " + ((this, currSub, outerSubst)))
460           if (ctx.debug) Thread.dumpStack()
461         }
462         else currSub = outerSubst >> rebindings
463       }
464 
465       /** The substitution that specifies the trees that compute the values of the subpattern binders.
466         *
467         * Should not be used to perform actual substitution!
468         * Only used to reason symbolically about the values the subpattern binders are bound to.
469         * See TreeMakerToCond#updateSubstitution.
470         *
471         * Overridden in PreserveSubPatBinders to pretend it replaces the subpattern binders by subpattern refs
472         * (Even though we don't do so anymore -- see SI-5158, SI-5739 and SI-6070.)
473         *
474         * TODO: clean this up, would be nicer to have some higher-level way to compute
475         * the binders bound by this tree maker and the symbolic values that correspond to them
476         */
477       def subPatternsAsRebindings: Rebindings = rebindings
478 
479       // build Tree that chains `next` after the current extractor
480       def chainBefore(next: Tree)(casegen: Casegen): Tree
481     }
482 
483     sealed trait NoNewBinders extends TreeMaker {
484       protected val introducedRebindings: Rebindings = NoRebindings
485     }

487     case class TrivialTreeMaker(tree: Tree) extends TreeMaker with NoNewBinders {
488       def pos = tree.pos
489 
490       def chainBefore(next: Tree)(casegen: Casegen): Tree = tree
491     }

493     case class BodyTreeMaker(body: Tree, matchPt: Type) extends TreeMaker with NoNewBinders {
494       def pos = body.pos
495 
496       def chainBefore(next: Tree)(casegen: Casegen): Tree = // assert(next eq EmptyTree)
497         /*atPos(body.pos)*/(casegen.one(body)) // since SubstOnly treemakers are dropped, need to do it here
498       override def toString = "B" + ((body, matchPt))
499     }
500 
501     /**
502      * In scalac for such block
503      *   x match {
504      *     case d => <body>
505      *   }
506      *
507      * d inside <body> was to be substitued by x.
508      *
509      * In dotty, SubstOnlyTreeMakers instead generate normal ValDef,
510      *   and does not create a new substitution.
511      *
512      * This was done for several reasons:
513      *  1) it is a lot easyer to Y-check,
514      *     as d type could be used in <body>.
515      *  2) it would simplify debugging of the generated code as
516      *     this works also for nested patterns, and previously they used unreadable names
517      *  3) It showed better(~30%), performance,
518      *     Rebuilding tree and propagating types was taking substantial time.
519      */
520     case class SubstOnlyTreeMaker(prevBinder: Symbol, nextBinder: Symbol) extends TreeMaker {
521       val pos = Positions.NoPosition
522 
523       val introducedRebindings = Rebindings(prevBinder, nextBinder)
524       def chainBefore(next: Tree)(casegen: Casegen): Tree = next
525       //override def toString = "S" + localSubstitution
526     }
527 
528     sealed abstract class FunTreeMaker extends TreeMaker {
529       val nextBinder: Symbol
530       def pos = nextBinder.pos
531     }
532 
533     sealed abstract class CondTreeMaker extends FunTreeMaker {
534       val prevBinder: Symbol
535       val nextBinderTp: Type
536       val cond: Tree
537       val res: Tree
538 
539       val nextBinder: Symbol
540       lazy val introducedRebindings = /*
541         if (nextBinder ne prevBinder) Rebindings(prevBinder, nextBinder)
542         else */ NoRebindings
543 
544       def chainBefore(next: Tree)(casegen: Casegen): Tree =
545         if (prevBinder ne nextBinder) // happens when typeTest is known to succeed
546           /*atPos(pos)(*/casegen.flatMapCond(cond, res, nextBinder, next)//)
547         else casegen.flatMapGuard(cond, next)
548     }

550     // unless we're optimizing, emit local variable bindings for all subpatterns of extractor/case class patterns
551     protected val debugInfoEmitVars = true //!settings.optimise.value
552 
553     /**
554      * Tree maker that captures sub pattern values during pattern match.
555      */
556     sealed trait PreserveSubPatBinders extends TreeMaker {
557       val subPatBinders: List[Symbol] // captured values
558       val subPatRefs: List[Tree] // trees that will replace references to subPatBinders
559       val ignoredSubPatBinders: Set[Symbol] // ignored as they aren't used in body of pattern
560 
561       // unless `debugInfoEmitVars`, this set should contain the bare minimum for correctness
562       // mutable case class fields need to be stored regardless (SI-5158, SI-6070) -- see override in ProductExtractorTreeMaker
563       // sub patterns bound to wildcard (_) are never stored as they can't be referenced
564       // dirty debuggers will have to get dirty to see the wildcards
565       lazy val storedBinders: Set[Symbol] =
566         (if (debugInfoEmitVars) subPatBinders.toSet else Set.empty) ++ extraStoredBinders -- ignoredSubPatBinders
567 
568       // e.g., mutable fields of a case class in ProductExtractorTreeMaker
569       def extraStoredBinders: Set[Symbol]
570 
571       def emitVars = storedBinders.nonEmpty
572 
573       lazy val storedSubsted = (subPatBinders, subPatRefs).zipped.partition{ case (sym, _) => storedBinders(sym) }
574 
575       def stored = storedSubsted._1
576 
577       def substed = storedSubsted._2
578 
579       // dd: this didn't yet trigger error. But I believe it would. if this causes double denition of symbol error this can be replaced with NoRebindings
580       protected lazy val introducedRebindings:  Rebindings = if (!emitVars) Rebindings(subPatBinders, subPatRefs)
581       else {
582         val (subPatBindersSubstituted, subPatRefsSubstituted) = substed.unzip
583         Rebindings(subPatBindersSubstituted.toList, subPatRefsSubstituted.toList)
584       }
585 
586       /** The substitution that specifies the trees that compute the values of the subpattern binders.
587         *
588         * We pretend to replace the subpattern binders by subpattern refs
589         * (Even though we don't do so anymore -- see SI-5158, SI-5739 and SI-6070.)
590         */
591       override def subPatternsAsRebindings =
592         Rebindings(subPatBinders, subPatRefs) >> super.subPatternsAsRebindings
593 
594       def bindSubPats(in: Tree): Tree =
595         if (!emitVars) in
596         else {
597           // binders in `subPatBindersStored` that are referenced by tree `in`
598           val usedBinders = new collection.mutable.HashSet[Symbol]()
599           // all potentially stored subpat binders
600           val potentiallyStoredBinders = stored.unzip._1.toSet
601           // compute intersection of all symbols in the tree `in` and all potentially stored subpat binders
602           new DeepFolder[Unit]((x: Unit, t: Tree) =>
603             if (potentiallyStoredBinders(t.symbol)) usedBinders += t.symbol).apply((), in)
604 
605           if (usedBinders.isEmpty) in
606           else {
607             // only store binders actually used
608             val (subPatBindersStored, subPatRefsStored) = stored.filter{case (b, _) => usedBinders(b)}.unzip
609 
610             Block((subPatBindersStored.toList, subPatRefsStored.toList).zipped.map((bind, ref) => {
611               // required in case original pattern had a more precise type
612               // eg case s@"foo" =>  would be otherwise translated to s with type String instead of String("foo")
613               def refTpeWiden = ref.tpe.widen
614               def bindInfoWiden = bind.info.widen
615               def loc = bind.showFullName
616               if (!(ref.tpe <:< bind.info.widen)) {
617                 ctx.debuglog(s"here ${bind.showFullName} expected: ${bindInfoWiden.show} got: ${refTpeWiden.show}")
618               }
619               val refCasted = ref.ensureConforms(bind.info)
620               ValDef(bind.asTerm, refCasted)
621             }), in)
622           }
623         }
624     }
625 
626     /**
627      * Make a TreeMaker that will result in an extractor call specified by `extractor`
628      * the next TreeMaker (here, we don't know which it'll be) is chained after this one by flatMap'ing
629      * a function with binder `nextBinder` over our extractor's result
630      * the function's body is determined by the next TreeMaker
631      * (furthermore, the interpretation of `flatMap` depends on the codegen instance we're using).
632      *
633      * The values for the subpatterns, as computed by the extractor call in `extractor`,
634      * are stored in local variables that re-use the symbols in `subPatBinders`.
635      * This makes extractor patterns more debuggable (SI-5739).
636      */
637     case class ExtractorTreeMaker(extractor: Tree, extraCond: Option[Tree], nextBinder: Symbol)(
638       val subPatBinders: List[Symbol],
639       val subPatRefs: List[Tree],
640       extractorReturnsBoolean: Boolean,
641       val checkedLength: Option[Int],
642       val prevBinder: Symbol,
643       val ignoredSubPatBinders: Set[Symbol]
644     ) extends FunTreeMaker with PreserveSubPatBinders {
645 
646       def extraStoredBinders: Set[Symbol] = Set()
647 
648       ctx.debuglog(s"""
649         |ExtractorTreeMaker($extractor, $extraCond, $nextBinder) {
650         |  $subPatBinders
651         |  $subPatRefs
652         |  $extractorReturnsBoolean
653         |  $checkedLength
654         |  $prevBinder
655         |  $ignoredSubPatBinders
656         |}""".stripMargin)
657 
658       def chainBefore(next: Tree)(casegen: Casegen): Tree = {
659         val condAndNext = extraCond match {
660           case Some(cond: Tree) =>
661             casegen.ifThenElseZero(cond, bindSubPats(next))
662           case _ =>
663             bindSubPats(next)
664         }
665 
666         if (extractorReturnsBoolean) casegen.flatMapCond(extractor, unitLiteral, nextBinder, condAndNext)
667         else casegen.flatMap(extractor, nextBinder, condAndNext) // getType?
668       }
669 
670       override def toString = "X" + ((extractor, nextBinder.name))
671     }
672 
673     object IrrefutableExtractorTreeMaker {
674       // will an extractor with unapply method of methodtype `tp` always succeed?
675       // note: this assumes the other side-conditions implied by the extractor are met
676       // (argument of the right type, length check succeeds for unapplySeq,...)
677       def irrefutableExtractorType(tp: Type): Boolean = tp.resultType.dealias match {
678         // case TypeRef(_, SomeClass, _) => true todo
679         // probably not useful since this type won't be inferred nor can it be written down (yet)
680         // case ConstantTrue => true todo
681         case _            => false
682       }
683 
684       def unapply(xtm: ExtractorTreeMaker): Option[(Tree, Symbol)] = xtm match {
685         case ExtractorTreeMaker(extractor, None, nextBinder) if irrefutableExtractorType(extractor.tpe) =>
686           Some((extractor, nextBinder))
687         case _ =>
688           None
689       }
690     }
691 
692     object TypeTestTreeMaker {
693       // factored out so that we can consistently generate other representations of the tree that implements the test
694       // (e.g. propositions for exhaustivity and friends, boolean for isPureTypeTest)
695       trait TypeTestCondStrategy {
696         type Result
697 
698         def outerTest(testedBinder: Symbol, expectedTp: Type): Result
699         // TODO: can probably always widen
700         def typeTest(testedBinder: Symbol, expectedTp: Type): Result
701         def nonNullTest(testedBinder: Symbol): Result
702         def equalsTest(pat: Tree, testedBinder: Symbol): Result
703         def eqTest(pat: Tree, testedBinder: Symbol): Result
704         def and(a: Result, b: Result): Result
705         def tru: Result
706       }
707 
708       object treeCondStrategy extends TypeTestCondStrategy {
709         type Result = Tree
710 
711         def and(a: Result, b: Result): Result                = a.select(defn.Boolean_&&).appliedTo(b)
712         def tru                                              = Literal(Constant(true))
713         def typeTest(testedBinder: Symbol, expectedTp: Type) = codegen._isInstanceOf(testedBinder, expectedTp)
714         def nonNullTest(testedBinder: Symbol)                = ref(testedBinder).select(defn.Object_ne).appliedTo(Literal(Constant(null)))
715         def equalsTest(pat: Tree, testedBinder: Symbol)      = codegen._equals(pat, testedBinder)
716         def eqTest(pat: Tree, testedBinder: Symbol)          = ref(testedBinder).select(defn.Object_eq).appliedTo(pat)
717 
718         def outerTest(testedBinder: Symbol, expectedTp: Type): Tree = {
719           val expectedOuter = expectedTp.normalizedPrefix match {
720             //case NoType          => Literal(Constant(true)) // fallback for SI-6183 todo?
721             case pre: SingletonType => singleton(pre)
722           }
723 
724           // ExplicitOuter replaces `Select(q, outerSym) OBJ_EQ expectedPrefix` by `Select(q, outerAccessor(outerSym.owner)) OBJ_EQ expectedPrefix`
725           // if there's an outer accessor, otherwise the condition becomes `true` -- TODO: can we improve needsOuterTest so there's always an outerAccessor?
726           // val outer = expectedTp.typeSymbol.newMethod(vpmName.outer, newFlags = SYNTHETIC | ARTIFACT) setInfo expectedTp.prefix
727 
728           val expectedClass = expectedTp.dealias.classSymbol.asClass
729           val test = codegen._asInstanceOf(testedBinder, expectedTp)
730           // TODO: Use nme.OUTER_SELECT, like the Inliner does?
731           val outerAccessorTested = ctx.atPhase(ctx.explicitOuterPhase.next) { implicit ctx =>
732             ExplicitOuter.ensureOuterAccessors(expectedClass)
733             test.select(ExplicitOuter.outerAccessor(expectedClass)).select(defn.Object_eq).appliedTo(expectedOuter)
734           }
735           outerAccessorTested
736         }
737       }
738 
739       /*object pureTypeTestChecker extends TypeTestCondStrategy {
740         type Result = Boolean
741 
742         def typeTest(testedBinder: Symbol, expectedTp: Type): Result  = true
743 
744         def outerTest(testedBinder: Symbol, expectedTp: Type): Result = false
745         def nonNullTest(testedBinder: Symbol): Result                 = false
746         def equalsTest(pat: Tree, testedBinder: Symbol): Result       = false
747         def eqTest(pat: Tree, testedBinder: Symbol): Result           = false
748         def and(a: Result, b: Result): Result                         = false // we don't and type tests, so the conjunction must include at least one false
749         def tru                                                       = true
750       }*/
751 
752       def nonNullImpliedByTestChecker(binder: Symbol) = new TypeTestCondStrategy {
753         type Result = Boolean
754 
755         def typeTest(testedBinder: Symbol, expectedTp: Type): Result  = testedBinder eq binder
756         def outerTest(testedBinder: Symbol, expectedTp: Type): Result = false
757         def nonNullTest(testedBinder: Symbol): Result                 = testedBinder eq binder
758         def equalsTest(pat: Tree, testedBinder: Symbol): Result       = false // could in principle analyse pat and see if it's statically known to be non-null
759         def eqTest(pat: Tree, testedBinder: Symbol): Result           = false // could in principle analyse pat and see if it's statically known to be non-null
760         def and(a: Result, b: Result): Result                         = a || b
761         def tru                                                       = false
762       }
763     }
764 
765     /** implements the run-time aspects of (8.2) (typedPattern has already done the necessary type transformations)
766       *
767       * Type patterns consist of types, type variables, and wildcards. A type pattern T is of one of the following forms:
768         - A reference to a class C, p.C, or T#C.
769           This type pattern matches any non-null instance of the given class.
770           Note that the prefix of the class, if it is given, is relevant for determining class instances.
771           For instance, the pattern p.C matches only instances of classes C which were created with the path p as prefix.
772           The bottom types scala.Nothing and scala.Null cannot be used as type patterns, because they would match nothing in any case.
773 
774         - A singleton type p.type.
775           This type pattern matches only the value denoted by the path p
776           (that is, a pattern match involved a comparison of the matched value with p using method eq in class AnyRef). // TODO: the actual pattern matcher uses ==, so that's what I'm using for now
777           // https://issues.scala-lang.org/browse/SI-4577 "pattern matcher, still disappointing us at equality time"
778 
779         - A compound type pattern T1 with ... with Tn where each Ti is a type pat- tern.
780           This type pattern matches all values that are matched by each of the type patterns Ti.
781 
782         - A parameterized type pattern T[a1,...,an], where the ai are type variable patterns or wildcards _.
783           This type pattern matches all values which match T for some arbitrary instantiation of the type variables and wildcards.
784           The bounds or alias type of these type variable are determined as described in (8.3).
785 
786         - A parameterized type pattern scala.Array[T1], where T1 is a type pattern. // TODO
787           This type pattern matches any non-null instance of type scala.Array[U1], where U1 is a type matched by T1.
788       **/
789     case class TypeTestTreeMaker(afterTest: Symbol, testedBinder: Symbol, expectedTp: Type, nextBinderTp: Type)(override val pos: Position, extractorArgTypeTest: Boolean = false) extends CondTreeMaker {
790       import TypeTestTreeMaker._
791 
792       ctx.debuglog("TTTM" + ((prevBinder, extractorArgTypeTest, testedBinder, expectedTp, nextBinderTp)))
793 
794       val prevBinder = testedBinder
795 
796       val nextBinder = afterTest.asTerm
797 
798       def outerTestNeeded(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean = {
799         // See the test for SI-7214 for motivation for dealias. Later `treeCondStrategy#outerTest`
800         // generates an outer test based on `patType.prefix` with automatically dealises.
801         expectedTp.dealias match {
802           case tref @ TypeRef(pre: SingletonType, _) =>
803             val s = tref
804             s.symbol.isClass &&
805             ExplicitOuter.needsOuterIfReferenced(s.symbol.asClass)
806           case _ =>
807             false
808         }
809       }
810 
811       override lazy val introducedRebindings = NoRebindings
812 
813       // the logic to generate the run-time test that follows from the fact that
814       // a `prevBinder` is expected to have type `expectedTp`
815       // the actual tree-generation logic is factored out, since the analyses generate Cond(ition)s rather than Trees
816       // TODO: `null match { x : T }` will yield a check that (indirectly) tests whether `null ne null`
817       // don't bother (so that we don't end up with the warning "comparing values of types Null and Null using `ne' will always yield false")
818       def renderCondition(cs: TypeTestCondStrategy): cs.Result = {
819         import cs._
820 
821         // propagate expected type
822         def expTp(t: Tree): t.type = t // setType expectedTp todo:
823 
824         def testedWide              = testedBinder.info.widen
825         def expectedWide            = expectedTp.widen
826         def isAnyRef                = testedWide <:< defn.AnyRefType
827         def isAsExpected            = testedWide <:< expectedTp
828         def isExpectedPrimitiveType = isAsExpected && expectedTp.classSymbol.isPrimitiveValueClass
829         def isExpectedReferenceType = isAsExpected && (expectedTp <:< defn.AnyRefType)
830         def mkNullTest              = nonNullTest(testedBinder)
831         def mkOuterTest             = outerTest(testedBinder, expectedTp)
832         def mkTypeTest              = typeTest(testedBinder, expectedWide)
833 
834         def mkEqualsTest(lhs: Tree): cs.Result      = equalsTest(lhs, testedBinder)
835         def mkEqTest(lhs: Tree): cs.Result          = eqTest(lhs, testedBinder)
836         def addOuterTest(res: cs.Result): cs.Result = if (outerTestNeeded) and(res, mkOuterTest) else res
837 
838         // If we conform to expected primitive type:
839         //   it cannot be null and cannot have an outer pointer. No further checking.
840         // If we conform to expected reference type:
841         //   have to test outer and non-null
842         // If we do not conform to expected type:
843         //   have to test type and outer (non-null is implied by successful type test)
844         def mkDefault = (
845           if (isExpectedPrimitiveType) tru
846           else addOuterTest(
847             if (isExpectedReferenceType) mkNullTest
848             else mkTypeTest
849           )
850         )
851 
852         // true when called to type-test the argument to an extractor
853         // don't do any fancy equality checking, just test the type
854         // TODO: verify that we don't need to special-case Array
855         // I think it's okay:
856         //  - the isInstanceOf test includes a test for the element type
857         //  - Scala's arrays are invariant (so we don't drop type tests unsoundly)
858         if (extractorArgTypeTest) mkDefault
859         else expectedTp match {
860           case ThisType(tref) if tref.symbol.flags is Flags.Module            =>
861             and(mkEqualsTest(ref(tref.symbol.companionModule)), mkTypeTest) // must use == to support e.g. List() == Nil
862           case ConstantType(Constant(null)) if isAnyRef => mkEqTest(expTp(Literal(Constant(null))))
863           case ConstantType(const)                      => mkEqualsTest(expTp(Literal(const)))
864           case t: SingletonType                         => mkEqTest(singleton(expectedTp)) // SI-4577, SI-4897
865           //case ThisType(sym)                            => mkEqTest(expTp(This(sym)))
866           case _                                        => mkDefault
867         }
868       }
869 
870       val cond = renderCondition(treeCondStrategy)
871       val res  = codegen._asInstanceOf(testedBinder, nextBinderTp)
872 
873       // is this purely a type test, e.g. no outer check, no equality tests (used in switch emission)
874       //def isPureTypeTest = renderCondition(pureTypeTestChecker)
875 
876       def impliesBinderNonNull(binder: Symbol): Boolean =
877       // @odersky: scalac is able to infer in this method that nonNullImpliedByTestChecker.Result,
878       // dotty instead infers type projection TreeMakers.this.TypeTestTreeMaker.TypeTestCondStrategy#Result
879       // which in turn doesn't typecheck in this method. Can you please explain why?
880       // dotty deviation
881         renderCondition(nonNullImpliedByTestChecker(binder)).asInstanceOf[Boolean]
882 
883       override def toString = "TT" + ((expectedTp, testedBinder.name, nextBinderTp))
884     }
885 
886     // need to substitute to deal with existential types -- TODO: deal with existentials better, don't substitute (see RichClass during quick.comp)
887     case class EqualityTestTreeMaker(prevBinder: Symbol, subpatBinder: Symbol, patTree: Tree, override val pos: Position) extends CondTreeMaker {
888       val nextBinderTp = patTree.tpe & prevBinder.info
889       val nextBinder = if (prevBinder eq subpatBinder) freshSym(pos, nextBinderTp) else subpatBinder
890 
891       // NOTE: generate `patTree == patBinder`, since the extractor must be in control of the equals method (also, patBinder may be null)
892       // equals need not be well-behaved, so don't intersect with pattern's (stabilized) type (unlike MaybeBoundTyped's accumType, where it's required)
893       val cond = codegen._equals(patTree, prevBinder)
894       val res  = ref(prevBinder).ensureConforms(nextBinderTp)
895       override def toString = "ET" + ((prevBinder.name, patTree))
896     }
897 
898     case class AlternativesTreeMaker(prevBinder: Symbol, var altss: List[List[TreeMaker]], pos: Position) extends TreeMaker with NoNewBinders {
899       // don't substitute prevBinder to nextBinder, a set of alternatives does not need to introduce a new binder, simply reuse the previous one
900 
901       override private[TreeMakers] def incorporateOuterRebinding(outerSubst: Rebindings): Unit = {
902         super.incorporateOuterRebinding(outerSubst)
903         altss = altss map (alts => propagateRebindings(alts, rebindings))
904       }
905 
906       def chainBefore(next: Tree)(codegenAlt: Casegen): Tree = {
907         /*atPos(pos)*/{
908           // one alternative may still generate multiple trees (e.g., an extractor call + equality test)
909           // (for now,) alternatives may not bind variables (except wildcards), so we don't care about the final substitution built internally by makeTreeMakers
910           val combinedAlts = altss map (altTreeMakers =>
911             ((casegen: Casegen) => combineExtractors(altTreeMakers :+ TrivialTreeMaker(casegen.one(Literal(Constant(true)))))(casegen))
912             )
913 
914           val findAltMatcher = codegenAlt.matcher(EmptyTree, NoSymbol, defn.BooleanType)(combinedAlts, Some((x: Symbol) => Literal(Constant(false))))
915           codegenAlt.ifThenElseZero(findAltMatcher, next)
916         }
917       }
918     }

920     case class GuardTreeMaker(guardTree: Tree) extends TreeMaker with NoNewBinders {
921       val pos = guardTree.pos
922 
923       def chainBefore(next: Tree)(casegen: Casegen): Tree = casegen.flatMapGuard(guardTree, next)
924       override def toString = "G(" + guardTree + ")"
925     }
926 
927     // combineExtractors changes the current substitution's of the tree makers in `treeMakers`
928     // requires propagateSubstitution(treeMakers) has been called
929     def combineExtractors(treeMakers: List[TreeMaker])(casegen: Casegen): Tree = {
930       val (testsMakers, guardAndBodyMakers) = treeMakers.span(t => !(t.isInstanceOf[NoNewBinders]))
931       val body = guardAndBodyMakers.foldRight(EmptyTree: Tree)((a, b) => a.chainBefore(b)(casegen))
932       val rebindings = guardAndBodyMakers.last.rebindings.emitValDefs
933       testsMakers.foldRight(Block(rebindings, body): Tree)((a, b) => a.chainBefore(b)(casegen))
934     }
935     // a foldLeft to accumulate the localSubstitution left-to-right
936     // unlike in scalace it does not drop SubstOnly tree makers,
937     // as there could be types having them as prefix
938     def propagateRebindings(treeMakers: List[TreeMaker], initial: Rebindings): List[TreeMaker] = {
939       var accumSubst: Rebindings = initial
940       treeMakers foreach { maker =>
941         maker incorporateOuterRebinding accumSubst
942         accumSubst = maker.rebindings
943       }
944       treeMakers
945     }
946 
947     // calls propagateSubstitution on the treemakers
948     def combineCases(scrut: Tree, scrutSym: Symbol, casesRaw: List[List[TreeMaker]], pt: Type, owner: Symbol, matchFailGenOverride: Option[Symbol => Tree]): Tree = {
949       // unlike in scalac SubstOnlyTreeMakers are maintained.
950       val casesRebindingPropagated = casesRaw map (propagateRebindings(_, NoRebindings))
951 
952       def matchFailGen = matchFailGenOverride orElse Some((arg: Symbol) => Throw(New(defn.MatchErrorType, List(ref(arg)))))
953 
954       ctx.debuglog("combining cases: " + (casesRebindingPropagated.map(_.mkString(" >> ")).mkString("{", "\n", "}")))
955 
956         val (suppression, requireSwitch): (Suppression, Boolean) =
957           /*if (settings.XnoPatmatAnalysis)*/ (Suppression.NoSuppression, false)
958           /*else scrut match {
959             case Typed(tree, tpt) =>
960               val suppressExhaustive = tpt.tpe hasAnnotation UncheckedClass
961               val supressUnreachable = tree match {
962                 case Ident(name) if name startsWith nme.CHECK_IF_REFUTABLE_STRING => true // SI-7183 don't warn for withFilter's that turn out to be irrefutable.
963                 case _ => false
964               }
965               val suppression = Suppression(suppressExhaustive, supressUnreachable)
966               // matches with two or fewer cases need not apply for switchiness (if-then-else will do)
967               val requireSwitch = treeInfo.isSwitchAnnotation(tpt.tpe) && casesNoSubstOnly.lengthCompare(2) > 0
968               (suppression, requireSwitch)
969             case _ =>
970               (Suppression.NoSuppression, false)
971           }*/
972 
973         emitSwitch(scrut, scrutSym, casesRebindingPropagated, pt, matchFailGenOverride, suppression.exhaustive).getOrElse{
974           if (requireSwitch) ctx.warning("could not emit switch for @switch annotated match", scrut.pos)
975 
976           if (casesRebindingPropagated nonEmpty) {
977             // before optimizing, check casesNoSubstOnly for presence of a default case,
978             // since DCE will eliminate trivial cases like `case _ =>`, even if they're the last one
979             // exhaustivity and reachability must be checked before optimization as well
980             // TODO: improve notion of trivial/irrefutable -- a trivial type test before the body still makes for a default case
981             //   ("trivial" depends on whether we're emitting a straight match or an exception, or more generally, any supertype of scrutSym.tpe is a no-op)
982             //   irrefutability checking should use the approximation framework also used for CSE, unreachability and exhaustivity checking
983             val synthCatchAll: Option[Symbol => Tree] =
984               if (casesRebindingPropagated.nonEmpty && {
985                 val nonTrivLast = casesRebindingPropagated.last
986                 nonTrivLast.nonEmpty && nonTrivLast.head.isInstanceOf[BodyTreeMaker]
987               }) None
988               else matchFailGen
989 
990             analyzeCases(scrutSym, casesRebindingPropagated, pt, suppression)
991 
992             val (cases, toHoist) = optimizeCases(scrutSym, casesRebindingPropagated, pt)
993 
994             val matchRes = codegen.matcher(scrut, scrutSym, pt)(cases.map(x => combineExtractors(x) _), synthCatchAll)
995 
996             if (toHoist isEmpty) matchRes else Block(toHoist, matchRes)
997           } else {
998             codegen.matcher(scrut, scrutSym, pt)(Nil, matchFailGen)
999           }
1000         }
1001       }
1002   }
1003

1007     override def optimizeCases(prevBinder: Symbol, cases: List[List[TreeMaker]], pt: Type): (List[List[TreeMaker]], List[Tree]) = {
1008       // TODO: do CSE on result of doDCE(prevBinder, cases, pt)
1009       val optCases = cases// todo: doCSE(prevBinder, cases, pt)
1010       val toHoist = Nil/*(
1011         for (treeMakers <- optCases)
1012         yield treeMakers.collect{case tm: ReusedCondTreeMaker => tm.treesToHoist}
1013         ).flatten.flatten.toList*/
1014       (optCases, toHoist)
1015     }
1016   }
