1018   trait MatchTranslator extends TreeMakers with ScalacPatternExpanders {
1019 
1020     def isVarPattern(pat: Tree): Boolean = pat match {
1021       case x: BackquotedIdent => false
1022       case x: Ident => x.name.isVariableName
1023       case _ => false
1024     }
1025 
1026     /** A conservative approximation of which patterns do not discern anything.
1027       * They are discarded during the translation.
1028       */
1029     object WildcardPattern {
1030       def unapply(pat: Tree): Boolean = pat match {
1031         case Typed(_, arg) if arg.tpe.isRepeatedParam => true
1032         case Bind(nme.WILDCARD, WildcardPattern()) => true // don't skip when binding an interesting symbol!
1033         case t if (tpd.isWildcardArg(t))           => true
1034         case x: Ident                              => isVarPattern(x)
1035         case Alternative(ps)                       => ps forall unapply
1036         case EmptyTree                             => true
1037         case _                                     => false
1038       }
1039     }
1040 
1041     object PatternBoundToUnderscore {
1042       def unapply(pat: Tree): Boolean = pat match {
1043         case Bind(nme.WILDCARD, _)                => true // don't skip when binding an interesting symbol!
1044         case Ident(nme.WILDCARD)                  => true
1045         case Alternative(ps)                      => ps forall unapply
1046         case Typed(PatternBoundToUnderscore(), _) => false // true // Dmitry: change in dotty. Type test will be performed and the field must be stored
1047         case _                                    => false
1048       }
1049     }
1050 
1051     object SymbolBound {
1052       def unapply(tree: Tree): Option[(Symbol, Tree)] = tree match {
1053         case Bind(_, expr) if tree.symbol.exists => Some(tree.symbol -> expr)
1054         case _                                   => None
1055       }
1056     }
1057 
1058     def newBoundTree(tree: Tree, pt: Type): BoundTree = tree match {
1059       case SymbolBound(sym, Typed(subpat, tpe)) => BoundTree(freshSym(tree.pos, pt, PatMatPiName), tree)
1060       case SymbolBound(sym, expr) => BoundTree(sym, expr)
1061       case _                      => BoundTree(freshSym(tree.pos, pt, PatMatPName), tree)
1062     }
1063 
1064     /*final*/ case class BoundTree(binder: Symbol, tree: Tree) {
1065       private lazy val extractor = ExtractorCall(tree, binder)
1066 
1067       def pos = tree.pos
1068       def tpe = binder.info.widenDealias
1069       def pt  = unbound match {
1070         // case Star(tpt)      => this glbWith seqType(tpt.tpe) dd todo:
1071         case TypeBound(tpe) => tpe
1072         case tree           => tree.tpe
1073       }
1074 
1075       def glbWith(other: Type) = ctx.typeComparer.glb(tpe :: other :: Nil)// .normalize
1076 
1077       object SymbolAndTypeBound {
1078         def unapply(tree: Tree): Option[(Symbol, Type)] = tree match {
1079           case SymbolBound(sym, Typed(_: UnApply, _)) => None // see comment in #189
1080           case SymbolBound(sym, TypeBound(tpe)) => Some(sym -> tpe)
1081           case TypeBound(tpe)                   => Some(binder -> tpe)
1082           case _                                => None
1083         }
1084       }
1085 
1086       object SymbolAndValueBound {
1087         def unapply(tree: Tree): Option[(Symbol, Tree)] = tree match {
1088           case SymbolBound(sym, ConstantPattern(const)) => Some(sym -> const)
1089           case _                                => None
1090         }
1091       }
1092 
1093       object TypeBound {
1094         def unapply(tree: Tree): Option[Type] = tree match {
1095           case Typed(_, arg) if !arg.tpe.isRepeatedParam => Some(tree.typeOpt)
1096           case _                                         => None
1097         }
1098       }
1099 
1100       object ConstantPattern {
1101         def unapply(tree: Tree): Option[Tree] = tree match {
1102           case Literal(Constant(_)) | Ident(_) | Select(_, _) | This(_) => Some(tree)
1103           case _ => None
1104         }
1105       }
1106 
1107       private def rebindTo(pattern: Tree) = BoundTree(binder, pattern)
1108       private def step(treeMakers: TreeMaker*)(subpatterns: BoundTree*): TranslationStep = TranslationStep(treeMakers.toList, subpatterns.toList)
1109 
1110       private def bindingStep(sub: Symbol, subpattern: Tree) = step(SubstOnlyTreeMaker(sub, binder))(rebindTo(subpattern))
1111       private def equalityTestStep(testedSymbol: Symbol, constantSymbol: Symbol, constant: Tree)
1112                                                              = step(EqualityTestTreeMaker(testedSymbol, constantSymbol, constant, pos))()
1113       private def typeTestStep(sub: Symbol, subPt: Type)     = step(TypeTestTreeMaker(sub, binder, subPt, sub.termRef)(pos))()
1114       private def alternativesStep(alts: List[Tree])         = step(AlternativesTreeMaker(binder, translatedAlts(alts), alts.head.pos))()
1115       private def translatedAlts(alts: List[Tree])           = alts map (alt => rebindTo(alt).translate())
1116       private def noStep()                                   = step()()
1117 
1118       private def unsupportedPatternMsg =
1119         i"unsupported pattern: ${tree.show} / $this (this is a scalac bug.)"
1120 
1121       // example check: List[Int] <:< ::[Int]
1122       private def extractorStep(): TranslationStep = {
1123         def paramType = extractor.aligner.wholeType
1124         import extractor.treeMaker
1125         // chain a type-testing extractor before the actual extractor call
1126         // it tests the type, checks the outer pointer and casts to the expected type
1127         // TODO: the outer check is mandated by the spec for case classes, but we do it for user-defined unapplies as well [SPEC]
1128         // (the prefix of the argument passed to the unapply must equal the prefix of the type of the binder)
1129         lazy val typeTest = TypeTestTreeMaker(freshSym(pos, paramType), binder, paramType, paramType)(pos, extractorArgTypeTest = true)
1130         // check whether typetest implies binder is not null,
1131         // even though the eventual null check will be on typeTest.nextBinder
1132         // it'll be equal to binder casted to paramType anyway (and the type test is on binder)
1133         def extraction: TreeMaker = treeMaker(typeTest.nextBinder, typeTest.impliesBinderNonNull(binder), pos, paramType)
1134 
1135         // paramType = the type expected by the unapply
1136         // TODO: paramType may contain unbound type params (run/t2800, run/t3530)
1137         val makers = (
1138           // Statically conforms to paramType
1139           if (tpe <:< paramType) treeMaker(binder, false, pos, tpe) :: Nil
1140           else typeTest :: extraction :: Nil
1141         )
1142         step(makers: _*)(extractor.subBoundTrees: _*)
1143       }
1144 
1145       // Summary of translation cases. I moved the excerpts from the specification further below so all
1146       // the logic can be seen at once.
1147       //
1148       // [1] skip wildcard trees -- no point in checking them
1149       // [2] extractor and constructor patterns
1150       // [3] replace subpatBinder by patBinder, as if the Bind was not there.
1151       //     It must be patBinder, as subpatBinder has the wrong info: even if the bind assumes a better type,
1152       //     this is not guaranteed until we cast
1153       // [4] typed patterns - a typed pattern never has any subtrees
1154       //     must treat Typed and Bind together -- we need to know the patBinder of the Bind pattern to get at the actual type
1155       // [5] literal and stable id patterns
1156       // [6] pattern alternatives
1157       // [7] symbol-less bind patterns - this happens in certain ill-formed programs, there'll be an error later
1158       //     don't fail here though (or should we?)
1159       def nextStep(): TranslationStep = tree match {
1160         case _: UnApply | _: Apply | Typed(_: UnApply | _: Apply, _)  => extractorStep()
1161         case SymbolAndTypeBound(sym, tpe)                             => typeTestStep(sym, tpe)
1162         case TypeBound(tpe)                                           => typeTestStep(binder, tpe)
1163         case SymbolBound(sym, expr)                                   => bindingStep(sym, expr)
1164         case WildcardPattern()                                        => noStep()
1165         case ConstantPattern(const)                                   => equalityTestStep(binder, binder, const)
1166         case Alternative(alts)                                        => alternativesStep(alts)
1167         case _                                                        => ctx.error(unsupportedPatternMsg, pos) ; noStep()
1168       }
1169       def translate(): List[TreeMaker] = nextStep() merge (_.translate())
1170 
1171       private def concreteType = tpe.bounds.hi
1172       private def unbound = unbind(tree)
1173       private def tpe_s = if (pt <:< concreteType) "" + pt else s"$pt (binder: $tpe)"
1174       private def at_s = unbound match {
1175         case WildcardPattern() => ""
1176         case pat               => s" @ $pat"
1177       }
1178       override def toString = s"${binder.name}: $tpe_s$at_s"
1179     }
1180 
1181     // a list of TreeMakers that encode `patTree`, and a list of arguments for recursive invocations of `translatePattern` to encode its subpatterns
1182     /*final*/ case class TranslationStep(makers: List[TreeMaker], subpatterns: List[BoundTree]) {
1183       def merge(f: BoundTree => List[TreeMaker]): List[TreeMaker] = makers ::: (subpatterns flatMap f)
1184       override def toString = if (subpatterns.isEmpty) "" else subpatterns.mkString("(", ", ", ")")
1185     }
1186 
1187     def isSyntheticDefaultCase(cdef: CaseDef) = cdef match {
1188       case CaseDef(Bind(nme.DEFAULT_CASE, _), EmptyTree, _) => true
1189       case _                                                => false
1190     }
1191 
1192     /** Implement a pattern match by turning its cases (including the implicit failure case)
1193       * into the corresponding (monadic) extractors, and combining them with the `orElse` combinator.
1194       *
1195       * For `scrutinee match { case1 ... caseN }`, the resulting tree has the shape
1196       * `runOrElse(scrutinee)(x => translateCase1(x).orElse(translateCase2(x)).....orElse(zero))`
1197       *
1198       * NOTE: the resulting tree is not type checked, nor are nested pattern matches transformed
1199       *   thus, you must typecheck the result (and that will in turn translate nested matches)
1200       *   this could probably be optimized... (but note that the matchStrategy must be solved for each nested patternmatch)
1201       */
1202     def translateMatch(match_ : Match): Tree = {
1203       val Match(sel, cases) = match_
1204 
1205       val selectorTp = sel.tpe.widen/*withoutAnnotations*/
1206 
1207       val selectorSym = freshSym(sel.pos, selectorTp, PatMatSelectorName)
1208 
1209       val (nonSyntheticCases, defaultOverride) = cases match {
1210         case init :+ last if isSyntheticDefaultCase(last) => (init, Some(((scrut: Symbol) => last.body)))
1211         case _                                            => (cases, None)
1212       }
1213 
1214 
1215       // checkMatchVariablePatterns(nonSyntheticCases) // only used for warnings
1216 
1217       // we don't transform after uncurry
1218       // (that would require more sophistication when generating trees,
1219       //  and the only place that emits Matches after typers is for exception handling anyway)
1220       /*if (phase.id >= currentRun.uncurryPhase.id)
1221         devWarning(s"running translateMatch past uncurry (at $phase) on $selector match $cases")*/
1222 
1223       ctx.debuglog("translating " + cases.mkString("{", "\n", "}"))
1224 
1225       //val start = if (Statistics.canEnable) Statistics.startTimer(patmatNanos) else null
1226 
1227       // when one of the internal cps-type-state annotations is present, strip all CPS annotations
1228       ///val origPt  = removeCPSFromPt(match_.tpe)
1229       // relevant test cases: pos/existentials-harmful.scala, pos/gadt-gilles.scala, pos/t2683.scala, pos/virtpatmat_exist4.scala
1230       // pt is the skolemized version
1231       val pt = match_.tpe.widen //repeatedToSeq(origPt)
1232 
1233       // val packedPt = repeatedToSeq(typer.packedType(match_, context.owner))
1234       selectorSym.setFlag(Flags.SyntheticCase)
1235 
1236       // pt = Any* occurs when compiling test/files/pos/annotDepMethType.scala  with -Xexperimental
1237       val combined = combineCases(sel, selectorSym, nonSyntheticCases map translateCase(selectorSym, pt), pt, ctx.owner, defaultOverride)
1238 
1239       // if (Statistics.canEnable) Statistics.stopTimer(patmatNanos, start)
1240       Block(List(ValDef(selectorSym, sel)), combined)
1241     }
1242 
1243     /**  The translation of `pat if guard => body` has two aspects:
1244       *     1) the substitution due to the variables bound by patterns
1245       *     2) the combination of the extractor calls using `flatMap`.
1246       *
1247       * 2) is easy -- it looks like: `translatePattern_1.flatMap(translatePattern_2....flatMap(translatePattern_N.flatMap(translateGuard.flatMap((x_i) => success(Xbody(x_i)))))...)`
1248       *     this must be right-leaning tree, as can be seen intuitively by considering the scope of bound variables:
1249       *     variables bound by pat_1 must be visible from the function inside the left-most flatMap right up to Xbody all the way on the right
1250       * 1) is tricky because translatePattern_i determines the shape of translatePattern_i + 1:
1251       *    zoom in on `translatePattern_1.flatMap(translatePattern_2)` for example -- it actually looks more like:
1252       *      `translatePattern_1(x_scrut).flatMap((x_1) => {y_i -> x_1._i}translatePattern_2)`
1253       *
1254       *    `x_1` references the result (inside the monad) of the extractor corresponding to `pat_1`,
1255       *    this result holds the values for the constructor arguments, which translatePattern_1 has extracted
1256       *    from the object pointed to by `x_scrut`. The `y_i` are the symbols bound by `pat_1` (in order)
1257       *    in the scope of the remainder of the pattern, and they must thus be replaced by:
1258       *      - (for 1-ary unapply) x_1
1259       *      - (for n-ary unapply, n > 1) selection of the i'th tuple component of `x_1`
1260       *      - (for unapplySeq) x_1.apply(i)
1261       *
1262       *    in the treemakers,
1263       *
1264       *    Thus, the result type of `translatePattern_i`'s extractor must conform to `M[(T_1,..., T_n)]`.
1265       *
1266       *    Operationally, phase 1) is a foldLeft, since we must consider the depth-first-flattening of
1267       *    the transformed patterns from left to right. For every pattern ast node, it produces a transformed ast and
1268       *    a function that will take care of binding and substitution of the next ast (to the right).
1269       *
1270       */
1271     def translateCase(scrutSym: Symbol, pt: Type)(caseDef: CaseDef): List[TreeMaker] = {
1272       val CaseDef(pattern, guard, body) = caseDef
1273       translatePattern(BoundTree(scrutSym, pattern)) ++ translateGuard(guard) :+ translateBody(body, pt)
1274     }
1275 
1276     def translatePattern(bound: BoundTree): List[TreeMaker] = bound.translate()
1277 
1278     def translateGuard(guard: Tree): List[TreeMaker] =
1279       if (guard == EmptyTree) Nil
1280       else List(GuardTreeMaker(guard))
1281 
1282     // TODO: 1) if we want to support a generalisation of Kotlin's patmat continue, must not hard-wire lifting into the monad (which is now done by codegen.one),
1283     // so that user can generate failure when needed -- use implicit conversion to lift into monad on-demand?
1284     // to enable this, probably need to move away from Option to a monad specific to pattern-match,
1285     // so that we can return Option's from a match without ambiguity whether this indicates failure in the monad, or just some result in the monad
1286     // 2) body.tpe is the type of the body after applying the substitution that represents the solution of GADT type inference
1287     // need the explicit cast in case our substitutions in the body change the type to something that doesn't take GADT typing into account
1288     def translateBody(body: Tree, matchPt: Type): TreeMaker =
1289       BodyTreeMaker(body, matchPt)
1290 
1291     // Some notes from the specification
1292 
1293     /*A constructor pattern is of the form c(p1, ..., pn) where n  0.
1294       It consists of a stable identifier c, followed by element patterns p1, ..., pn.
1295       The constructor c is a simple or qualified name which denotes a case class (5.3.2).
1296 
1297       If the case class is monomorphic, then it must conform to the expected type of the pattern,
1298       and the formal parameter types of xs primary constructor (5.3) are taken as the expected
1299       types of the element patterns p1, ..., pn.
1300 
1301       If the case class is polymorphic, then its type parameters are instantiated so that the
1302       instantiation of c conforms to the expected type of the pattern.
1303       The instantiated formal parameter types of cs primary constructor are then taken as the
1304       expected types of the component patterns p1, ..., pn.
1305 
1306       The pattern matches all objects created from constructor invocations c(v1, ..., vn)
1307       where each element pattern pi matches the corresponding value vi .
1308       A special case arises when cs formal parameter types end in a repeated parameter.
1309       This is further discussed in (8.1.9).
1310     **/
1311 
1312     /* A typed pattern x : T consists of a pattern variable x and a type pattern T.
1313        The type of x is the type pattern T, where each type variable and wildcard is replaced by a fresh, unknown type.
1314        This pattern matches any value matched by the type pattern T (8.2); it binds the variable name to that value.
1315     */
1316 
1317     /* A pattern binder x@p consists of a pattern variable x and a pattern p.
1318        The type of the variable x is the static type T of the pattern p.
1319        This pattern matches any value v matched by the pattern p,
1320        provided the run-time type of v is also an instance of T,  <-- TODO! https://issues.scala-lang.org/browse/SI-1503
1321        and it binds the variable name to that value.
1322     */
1323 
1324     /* 8.1.4 Literal Patterns
1325          A literal pattern L matches any value that is equal (in terms of ==) to the literal L.
1326          The type of L must conform to the expected type of the pattern.
1327 
1328        8.1.5 Stable Identifier Patterns  (a stable identifier r (see 3.1))
1329          The pattern matches any value v such that r == v (12.1).
1330          The type of r must conform to the expected type of the pattern.
1331     */
1332 
1333 
1334     ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
1335     // helper methods: they analyze types and trees in isolation, but they are not (directly) concerned with the structure of the overall translation
1336     ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
1337 
1338     object ExtractorCall {
1339       // TODO: check unargs == args
1340       def apply(tree: Tree, binder: Symbol): ExtractorCall = {
1341         tree match {
1342           case Typed(unapply, _) => apply(unapply, binder)
1343           case UnApply(unfun, implicits, args) =>
1344             val mt @ MethodType(_) = unfun.tpe.widen
1345             val castedBinder = ref(binder).ensureConforms(mt.paramInfos.head)
1346             var synth = unfun.appliedTo(castedBinder)
1347             if (implicits.nonEmpty) synth = synth.appliedToArgs(implicits)
1348             new ExtractorCallRegular(alignPatterns(tree, synth.tpe), synth, args, synth.tpe)
1349         }
1350       }
1351     }
1352 
1353     abstract class ExtractorCall(val aligner: PatternAligned) {
1354 
1355       import aligner._
1356 
1357       def args: List[Tree]
1358 
1359       // don't go looking for selectors if we only expect one pattern
1360       def rawSubPatTypes = aligner.extractedTypes
1361 
1362       def typeArgOfBaseTypeOr(tp: Type, baseClass: Symbol)(or: => Type): Type = (tp.baseType(baseClass)).argInfos match {
1363         case x :: Nil => x
1364         case _        => or
1365       }
1366 
1367       def resultInMonad  =
1368         if (aligner.isBool) defn.UnitType
1369         else if (isProductMatch(resultType, aligner.prodArity)) resultType
1370         else if (isGetMatch(resultType)) extractorMemberType(resultType, nme.get)
1371         else resultType
1372 
1373       def resultType: Type
1374 
1375       /** Create the TreeMaker that embodies this extractor call
1376         *
1377         * `binder` has been casted to `paramType` if necessary
1378         * `binderKnownNonNull` indicates whether the cast implies `binder` cannot be null
1379         * when `binderKnownNonNull` is `true`, `ProductExtractorTreeMaker` does not do a (redundant) null check on binder
1380         */
1381       def treeMaker(binder: Symbol, binderKnownNonNull: Boolean, pos: Position, binderTypeTested: Type): TreeMaker
1382 
1383       // `subPatBinders` are the variables bound by this pattern in the following patterns
1384       // subPatBinders are replaced by references to the relevant part of the extractor's result (tuple component, seq element, the result as-is)
1385       // must set infos to `subPatTypes`, which are provided by extractor's result,
1386       // as b.info may be based on a Typed type ascription, which has not been taken into account yet by the translation
1387       // (it will later result in a type test when `tp` is not a subtype of `b.info`)
1388       // TODO: can we simplify this, together with the Bound case?
1389       def subPatBinders = subBoundTrees map (_.binder)
1390       lazy val subBoundTrees = (args, subPatTypes).zipped map newBoundTree
1391 
1392       // never store these in local variables (for PreserveSubPatBinders)
1393       lazy val ignoredSubPatBinders: Set[Symbol] = subPatBinders zip args collect { case (b, PatternBoundToUnderscore()) => b } toSet
1394 
1395       // do repeated-parameter expansion to match up with the expected number of arguments (in casu, subpatterns)
1396       private def nonStarSubPatTypes = aligner.typedNonStarPatterns map (_.tpe)
1397 
1398       def subPatTypes: List[Type] = typedPatterns map (_.tpe)
1399 
1400       // there are `prodArity` non-seq elements in the tuple.
1401       protected def firstIndexingBinder = prodArity
1402       protected def expectedLength      = elementArity
1403       protected def lastIndexingBinder  = totalArity - starArity - 1
1404 
1405       private def productElemsToN(binder: Symbol, n: Int): List[Tree] = 1 to n map tupleSel(binder) toList
1406       private def genTake(binder: Symbol, n: Int): List[Tree]         = (0 until n).toList map (codegen index seqTree(binder))
1407       private def genDrop(binder: Symbol, n: Int): List[Tree]         = codegen.drop(seqTree(binder))(expectedLength) :: Nil
1408 
1409       // codegen.drop(seqTree(binder))(nbIndexingIndices)))).toList
1410       protected def seqTree(binder: Symbol)                = tupleSel(binder)(firstIndexingBinder + 1)
1411       protected def tupleSel(binder: Symbol)(i: Int): Tree = {
1412         val accessors =
1413           if (defn.isProductSubType(binder.info))
1414             productSelectors(binder.info)
1415           else binder.caseAccessors
1416         val res =
1417           if (accessors.isDefinedAt(i - 1)) ref(binder).select(accessors(i - 1).name)
1418           else codegen.tupleSel(binder)(i) // this won't type check for case classes, as they do not inherit ProductN
1419         val rsym = res.symbol // just for debugging
1420         res
1421       }
1422 
1423       // the trees that select the subpatterns on the extractor's result,
1424       // referenced by `binder`
1425       protected def subPatRefsSeq(binder: Symbol): List[Tree] = {
1426         def lastTrees: List[Tree] = (
1427           if (!aligner.isStar) Nil
1428           else if (expectedLength == 0) seqTree(binder) :: Nil
1429           else genDrop(binder, expectedLength)
1430         )
1431         // this error-condition has already been checked by checkStarPatOK:
1432         //   if (isSeq) assert(firstIndexingBinder + nbIndexingIndices + (if (lastIsStar) 1 else 0) == totalArity, "(resultInMonad, ts, subPatTypes, subPats)= " +(resultInMonad, ts, subPatTypes, subPats))
1433 
1434         // [1] there are `firstIndexingBinder` non-seq tuple elements preceding the Seq
1435         // [2] then we have to index the binder that represents the sequence for the remaining subpatterns, except for...
1436         // [3] the last one -- if the last subpattern is a sequence wildcard:
1437         //       drop the prefix (indexed by the refs on the preceding line), return the remainder
1438         (    productElemsToN(binder, firstIndexingBinder)
1439           ++ genTake(binder, expectedLength)
1440           ++ lastTrees
1441         ).toList
1442       }
1443 
1444       // the trees that select the subpatterns on the extractor's result, referenced by `binder`
1445       // require (nbSubPats > 0 && (!lastIsStar || isSeq))
1446       protected def subPatRefs(binder: Symbol): List[Tree] = {
1447         val refs = if (totalArity > 0 && isSeq) subPatRefsSeq(binder)
1448         else if (binder.info.member(nme._1).exists && !isSeq) productElemsToN(binder, totalArity)
1449         else ref(binder) :: Nil
1450         refs
1451       }
1452 
1453       val mathSignymSymbol = defn.ScalaMathPackageVal.requiredMethod("signum".toTermName, List(defn.IntType))
1454       val mathSignum = ref(defn.ScalaMathPackageVal).select(mathSignymSymbol)
1455 
1456 
1457       private def compareInts(t1: Tree, t2: Tree) =
1458         mathSignum.appliedTo(t1.select(defn.Int_-).appliedTo(t2))
1459         //gen.mkMethodCall(termMember(ScalaPackage, "math"), TermName("signum"), Nil, (t1 INT_- t2) :: Nil)
1460 
1461       protected def lengthGuard(binder: Symbol): Option[Tree] =
1462       // no need to check unless it's an unapplySeq and the minimal length is non-trivially satisfied
1463         checkedLength map { expectedLength =>
1464           // `binder.lengthCompare(expectedLength)`
1465           // ...if binder has a lengthCompare method, otherwise
1466           // `scala.math.signum(binder.length - expectedLength)`
1467           def checkExpectedLength: Tree = sequenceType.member(nme.lengthCompare) match {
1468             case NoDenotation => compareInts(Select(seqTree(binder), nme.length), Literal(Constant(expectedLength)))
1469             case x:SingleDenotation   => (seqTree(binder).select(x.symbol)).appliedTo(Literal(Constant(expectedLength)))
1470             case _ =>
1471               ctx.error("TODO: multiple lengthCompare")
1472               EmptyTree
1473           }
1474 
1475           // the comparison to perform
1476           // when the last subpattern is a wildcard-star the expectedLength is but a lower bound
1477           // (otherwise equality is required)
1478           def compareOp: (Tree, Tree) => Tree =
1479             if (aligner.isStar) _.select(defn.Int_>=).appliedTo(_)
1480             else _.select(defn.Int_==).appliedTo(_)
1481 
1482           // `if (binder != null && $checkExpectedLength [== | >=] 0) then else zero`
1483           (seqTree(binder).select(defn.Any_!=).appliedTo(Literal(Constant(null)))).select(defn.Boolean_&&).appliedTo(compareOp(checkExpectedLength, Literal(Constant(0))))
1484         }
1485 
1486       def checkedLength: Option[Int] =
1487       // no need to check unless it's an unapplySeq and the minimal length is non-trivially satisfied
1488         if (!isSeq || expectedLength < starArity) None
1489         else Some(expectedLength)
1490     }
1491 
1492     class ExtractorCallRegular(aligner: PatternAligned, extractorCallIncludingDummy: Tree, val args: List[Tree], val resultType: Type) extends ExtractorCall(aligner) {
1493 
1494       /** Create the TreeMaker that embodies this extractor call
1495         *
1496         *  `binder` has been casted to `paramType` if necessary
1497         *  `binderKnownNonNull` is not used in this subclass
1498         *
1499         *  TODO: implement review feedback by @retronym:
1500         *    Passing the pair of values around suggests:
1501         *       case class Binder(sym: Symbol, knownNotNull: Boolean).
1502         *    Perhaps it hasn't reached critical mass, but it would already clean things up a touch.
1503         */
1504       def treeMaker(patBinderOrCasted: Symbol, binderKnownNonNull: Boolean, pos: Position, binderTypeTested: Type): TreeMaker = {
1505         // the extractor call (applied to the binder bound by the flatMap corresponding
1506         // to the previous (i.e., enclosing/outer) pattern)
1507         val extractorApply = extractorCallIncludingDummy// spliceApply(patBinderOrCasted)
1508         // can't simplify this when subPatBinders.isEmpty, since UnitTpe is definitely
1509         // wrong when isSeq, and resultInMonad should always be correct since it comes
1510         // directly from the extractor's result type
1511         val binder = freshSym(pos, resultInMonad)
1512         val spb = subPatBinders
1513         ExtractorTreeMaker(extractorApply, lengthGuard(binder), binder)(
1514           spb,
1515           subPatRefs(binder, spb, resultType),
1516           aligner.isBool,
1517           checkedLength,
1518           patBinderOrCasted,
1519           ignoredSubPatBinders
1520         )
1521       }
1522 
1523       override protected def seqTree(binder: Symbol): Tree =
1524         if (firstIndexingBinder == 0) ref(binder)
1525         else super.seqTree(binder)
1526 
1527       // the trees that select the subpatterns on the extractor's result, referenced by `binder`
1528       // require (totalArity > 0 && (!lastIsStar || isSeq))
1529       protected def subPatRefs(binder: Symbol, subpatBinders: List[Symbol], binderTypeTested: Type): List[Tree] = {
1530         if (aligner.isSingle && aligner.extractor.prodArity == 1 && defn.isTupleType(binder.info)) {
1531           // special case for extractor
1532           // comparing with scalac additional assertions added
1533           val subpw = subpatBinders.head.info.widen
1534           val binderw = binder.info.widen
1535           val go = subpatBinders.head.info <:< binder.info
1536           val go1 = binder.info <:< subpatBinders.head.info
1537           //val spr = subPatRefs(binder)
1538           assert(go && go1)
1539           ref(binder) :: Nil
1540         }
1541         else if ((aligner.isSingle && aligner.extractor.prodArity == 1) &&
1542                  !isProductMatch(binderTypeTested, aligner.prodArity) && isGetMatch(binderTypeTested))
1543           List(ref(binder))
1544         else
1545           subPatRefs(binder)
1546       }
1547 
1548       /*protected def spliceApply(binder: Symbol): Tree = {
1549         object splice extends TreeMap {

1551             ref(binder) //setPos pos

1553           override def transform(t: tpd.Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): tpd.Tree = t match {
1554             // duplicated with the extractor Unapplied
1555             case Apply(x, List(i @ Ident(nme.SELECTOR_DUMMY))) =>
1556               cpy.Apply(t, x, binderRef(i.pos) :: Nil)

1558             case Apply(x, List(i @ (sel @ Select(Ident(nme.SELECTOR_DUMMY), name)))) =>
1559               cpy.Apply(t, x, cpy.Select(sel, binderRef(i.pos), name) :: Nil)
1560             case _ =>
1561               super.transform(t)
1562           }

1566 
1567       override def rawSubPatTypes = aligner.extractor.varargsTypes
1568     }
1569   }
1570 
1571   /** An extractor returns: F1, F2, ..., Fi, opt[Seq[E] or E*]
1572     *        A case matches: P1, P2, ..., Pj, opt[Seq[E]]
1573     *          Put together: P1/F1, P2/F2, ... Pi/Fi, Pi+1/E, Pi+2/E, ... Pj/E, opt[Seq[E]]
1574     *
1575     *  Here Pm/Fi is the last pattern to match the fixed arity section.
1576     *
1577     *    prodArity: the value of i, i.e. the number of non-sequence types in the extractor
1578     *    nonStarArity: the value of j, i.e. the number of non-star patterns in the case definition
1579     *    elementArity: j - i, i.e. the number of non-star patterns which must match sequence elements
1580     *       starArity: 1 or 0 based on whether there is a star (sequence-absorbing) pattern
1581     *      totalArity: nonStarArity + starArity, i.e. the number of patterns in the case definition
1582     *
1583     *  Note that prodArity is a function only of the extractor, and
1584     *  nonStar/star/totalArity are all functions of the patterns. The key
1585     *  value for aligning and typing the patterns is elementArity, as it
1586     *  is derived from both sets of information.
1587     */
1588   trait PatternExpander[Pattern, Type] {
1589     /** You'll note we're not inside the cake. "Pattern" and "Type" are
1590       *  arbitrary types here, and NoPattern and NoType arbitrary values.
1591       */
1592     def NoPattern: Pattern
1593     def NoType: Type
1594 
1595     /** It's not optimal that we're carrying both sequence and repeated
1596       *  type here, but the implementation requires more unraveling before
1597       *  it can be avoided.
1598       *
1599       *  sequenceType is Seq[T], elementType is T, repeatedType is T*.
1600       */
1601     sealed case class Repeated(sequenceType: Type, elementType: Type, repeatedType: Type) {
1602       def exists = elementType != NoType
1603 
1604       def elementList  = if (exists) elementType :: Nil else Nil
1605       def sequenceList = if (exists) sequenceType :: Nil else Nil
1606       def repeatedList = if (exists) repeatedType :: Nil else Nil
1607 
1608       override def toString = s"${elementType}*"
1609     }
1610     object NoRepeated extends Repeated(NoType, NoType, NoType) {
1611       override def toString = "<none>"
1612     }
1613 
1614     /*final*/ case class Patterns(fixed: List[Pattern], star: Pattern) {
1615       def hasStar      = star != NoPattern
1616       def starArity    = if (hasStar) 1 else 0
1617       def nonStarArity = fixed.length
1618       def totalArity   = nonStarArity + starArity
1619       def starPatterns = if (hasStar) star :: Nil else Nil
1620       def all          = fixed ::: starPatterns
1621 
1622       override def toString = all mkString ", "
1623     }
1624 
1625     /** An 'extractor' can be a case class or an unapply or unapplySeq method.
1626       *  Decoding what it is that they extract takes place before we arrive here,
1627       *  so that this class can concentrate only on the relationship between
1628       *  patterns and types.
1629       *
1630       *  In a case class, the class is the unextracted type and the fixed and
1631       *  repeated types are derived from its constructor parameters.
1632       *
1633       *  In an unapply, this is reversed: the parameter to the unapply is the
1634       *  unextracted type, and the other types are derived based on the return
1635       *  type of the unapply method.
1636       *
1637       *  In other words, this case class and unapply are encoded the same:
1638       *
1639       *    case class Foo(x: Int, y: Int, zs: Char*)
1640       *    def unapplySeq(x: Foo): Option[(Int, Int, Seq[Char])]
1641       *
1642       *  Both are Extractor(Foo, Int :: Int :: Nil, Repeated(Seq[Char], Char, Char*))
1643       *
1644       *  @param  whole     The type in its unextracted form
1645       *  @param  fixed     The non-sequence types which are extracted
1646       *  @param  repeated  The sequence type which is extracted
1647       */
1648     /*final*/ case class Extractor(whole: Type, fixed: List[Type], repeated: Repeated) {
1649       require(whole != NoType, s"expandTypes($whole, $fixed, $repeated)")
1650 
1651       def prodArity    = fixed.length
1652       def hasSeq       = repeated.exists
1653       def elementType  = repeated.elementType
1654       def sequenceType = repeated.sequenceType
1655       def allTypes     = fixed ::: repeated.sequenceList
1656       def varargsTypes = fixed ::: repeated.repeatedList
1657       def isErroneous  = allTypes contains NoType
1658 
1659       private def typeStrings = fixed.map("" + _) ::: ( if (hasSeq) List("" + repeated) else Nil )
1660 
1661       def offeringString = if (isErroneous) "<error>" else typeStrings match {
1662         case Nil       => "Boolean"
1663         case tp :: Nil => tp
1664         case tps       => tps.mkString("(", ", ", ")")
1665       }
1666       override def toString = "%s => %s".format(whole, offeringString)
1667     }
1668 
1669     /*final*/ case class TypedPat(pat: Pattern, tpe: Type) {
1670       override def toString = s"$pat: $tpe"
1671     }
1672 
1673     /** If elementArity is...
1674       *    0: A perfect match between extractor and the fixed patterns.
1675       *       If there is a star pattern it will match any sequence.
1676       *  > 0: There are more patterns than products. There will have to be a
1677       *       sequence which can populate at least <elementArity> patterns.
1678       *  < 0: There are more products than patterns: compile time error.
1679       */
1680     /*final*/ case class Aligned(patterns: Patterns, extractor: Extractor) {
1681       def elementArity = patterns.nonStarArity - prodArity
1682       def prodArity    = extractor.prodArity
1683       def starArity    = patterns.starArity
1684       def totalArity   = patterns.totalArity
1685 
1686       def wholeType            = extractor.whole
1687       def sequenceType         = extractor.sequenceType
1688       def productTypes         = extractor.fixed
1689       def extractedTypes       = extractor.allTypes
1690       def typedNonStarPatterns = products ::: elements
1691       def typedPatterns        = typedNonStarPatterns ::: stars
1692 
1693       def isBool   = !isSeq && prodArity == 0
1694       def isSingle = !isSeq && totalArity == 1
1695       def isStar   = patterns.hasStar
1696       def isSeq    = extractor.hasSeq
1697 
1698       private def typedAsElement(pat: Pattern)  = TypedPat(pat, extractor.elementType)
1699       private def typedAsSequence(pat: Pattern) = TypedPat(pat, extractor.sequenceType)
1700       private def productPats = patterns.fixed take prodArity
1701       private def elementPats = patterns.fixed drop prodArity
1702       private def products    = (productPats, productTypes).zipped map TypedPat
1703       private def elements    = elementPats map typedAsElement
1704       private def stars       = patterns.starPatterns map typedAsSequence
1705 
1706       override def toString = s"""
1707       |Aligned {
1708       |   patterns  $patterns
1709       |  extractor  $extractor
1710       |    arities  $prodArity/$elementArity/$starArity  // product/element/star
1711       |      typed  ${typedPatterns mkString ", "}
1712       |}""".stripMargin.trim
1713     }
1714   }
1715 
1716   /** This is scalac-specific logic layered on top of the scalac-agnostic
1717     *  "matching products to patterns" logic defined in PatternExpander.
1718     */
1719   trait ScalacPatternExpanders {
1720 
1721     type PatternAligned = ScalacPatternExpander#Aligned
1722 
1723     implicit class AlignedOps(val aligned: PatternAligned) {
1724       import aligned._
1725       def expectedTypes     = typedPatterns map (_.tpe)
1726       def unexpandedFormals = extractor.varargsTypes
1727     }
1728 
1729     trait ScalacPatternExpander extends PatternExpander[Tree, Type] {
1730       def NoPattern = EmptyTree
1731       def NoType    = core.Types.NoType
1732 
1733       def newPatterns(patterns: List[Tree]): Patterns = patterns match {
1734         case init :+ last if tpd.isWildcardStarArg(last) => Patterns(init, last)
1735         case _                            => Patterns(patterns, NoPattern)
1736       }
1737       def typeOfMemberNamedHead(tpe: Type): Type = tpe.select(nme.head)
1738       def typeOfMemberNamedApply(tpe: Type): Type = tpe.select(nme.apply)
1739 
1740       def elementTypeOf(tpe: Type) = {
1741         val seq = tpe //repeatedToSeq(tpe)
1742 
1743         ( typeOfMemberNamedHead(seq)
1744           orElse typeOfMemberNamedApply(seq)
1745           orElse seq.elemType
1746         )
1747       }
1748       def newExtractor(whole: Type, fixed: List[Type], repeated: Repeated): Extractor = {
1749         ctx.log(s"newExtractor($whole, $fixed, $repeated")
1750         Extractor(whole, fixed, repeated)
1751       }
1752 
1753       // Turn Seq[A] into Repeated(Seq[A], A, A*)
1754       def repeatedFromSeq(seqType: Type): Repeated = {
1755         val elem     = elementTypeOf(seqType)
1756         val repeated = /*scalaRepeatedType(*/elem//)
1757 
1758         Repeated(seqType, elem, repeated)
1759       }
1760       // Turn A* into Repeated(Seq[A], A, A*)
1761       def repeatedFromVarargs(repeated: Type): Repeated =
1762         //Repeated(repeatedToSeq(repeated), repeatedToSingle(repeated), repeated)
1763         Repeated(repeated, repeated.elemType, repeated)
1764 
1765       /** In this case we are basing the pattern expansion on a case class constructor.
1766         *  The argument is the MethodType carried by the primary constructor.
1767         */
1768       def applyMethodTypes(method: Type): Extractor = {
1769         val whole = method.finalResultType
1770 
1771         method.paramInfoss.head match {
1772           case init :+ last if last.isRepeatedParam => newExtractor(whole, init, repeatedFromVarargs(last))
1773           case tps                                  => newExtractor(whole, tps, NoRepeated)
1774         }
1775       }
1776 
1777       def hasSelectors(tpe: Type) = tpe.member(nme._1).exists && tpe.member(nme._2).exists // dd todo: ???
1778 
1779 
1780       /** In this case, expansion is based on an unapply or unapplySeq method.
1781         *  Unfortunately the MethodType does not carry the information of whether
1782         *  it was unapplySeq, so we have to funnel that information in separately.
1783         */
1784       def unapplyMethodTypes(tree: Tree, fun: Tree, args: List[Tree], resultType: Type, isSeq: Boolean): Extractor = {
1785         _id = _id + 1
1786 
1787         val whole       = tree.tpe // see scaladoc for Trees.Unapply
1788               // fun.tpe.widen.paramTypess.headOption.flatMap(_.headOption).getOrElse(NoType)//firstParamType(method)
1789         val resultOfGet = extractorMemberType(resultType, nme.get)
1790 
1791         val expanded: List[Type] = /*(
1792           if (result =:= defn.BooleanType) Nil
1793           else if (defn.isProductSubType(result)) productSelectorTypes(result)
1794           else if (result.classSymbol is Flags.CaseClass) result.decls.filter(x => x.is(Flags.CaseAccessor) && x.is(Flags.Method)).map(_.info).toList
1795           else result.select(nme.get) :: Nil
1796           )*/
1797           if (isProductMatch(resultType, args.length)) productSelectorTypes(resultType)
1798           else if (isGetMatch(resultType)) getUnapplySelectors(resultOfGet, args)
1799           else if (resultType isRef defn.BooleanClass) Nil
1800           else {
1801             ctx.error(i"invalid return type in Unapply node: $resultType")
1802             Nil
1803           }
1804 
1805         expanded match {
1806           case init :+ last if isSeq => newExtractor(whole, init, repeatedFromSeq(last))
1807           case tps                   => newExtractor(whole, tps, NoRepeated)
1808         }
1809       }
1810     }
1811 
1812     object alignPatterns extends ScalacPatternExpander {
1813       private def validateAligned(tree: Tree, aligned: Aligned): Aligned = {
1814         import aligned._
1815 
1816         def owner         = tree.symbol.owner
1817         def offering      = extractor.offeringString
1818         def symString     = tree.symbol.showLocated
1819         def offerString   = if (extractor.isErroneous) "" else s" offering $offering"
1820         def arityExpected = (if (extractor.hasSeq) "at least " else "") + prodArity
1821 
1822         def err(msg: String)         = ctx.error(msg, tree.pos)
1823         def warn(msg: String)        = ctx.warning(msg, tree.pos)
1824         def arityError(what: String) = err(s"${_id} $what patterns for $owner$offerString: expected $arityExpected, found $totalArity")
1825 
1826         if (isStar && !isSeq)
1827           err("Star pattern must correspond with varargs or unapplySeq")
1828         else if (elementArity < 0)
1829           arityError("not enough")
1830         else if (elementArity > 0 && !extractor.hasSeq)
1831           arityError("too many")
1832 
1833         aligned
1834       }
1835 
1836       object Applied {
1837         // Duplicated with `spliceApply`
1838         def unapply(tree: Tree): Option[Tree] = tree match {
1839           // SI-7868 Admit Select() to account for numeric widening, e.g. <unappplySelector>.toInt
1840           /*case Apply(fun, (Ident(nme.SELECTOR_DUMMY)| Select(Ident(nme.SELECTOR_DUMMY), _)) :: Nil)
1841           => Some(fun)*/
1842           case Apply(fun, _) => unapply(fun)
1843           case _             => None
1844         }
1845       }
1846 
1847       def apply(tree: Tree, sel: Tree, args: List[Tree], resultType: Type): Aligned = {
1848         val fn = sel match {
1849           case Applied(fn) => fn
1850           case _           => sel
1851         }
1852         val patterns  = newPatterns(args)
1853         val isSeq = sel.symbol.name == nme.unapplySeq
1854         val extractor = sel.symbol.name match {
1855           case nme.unapply    => unapplyMethodTypes(tree, /*fn*/sel, args, resultType, isSeq = false)
1856           case nme.unapplySeq => unapplyMethodTypes(tree, /*fn*/sel, args, resultType, isSeq = true)
1857           case _              => applyMethodTypes(/*fn*/sel.tpe)
1858         }
1859 
1860         validateAligned(fn, Aligned(patterns, extractor))
1861       }
1862 
1863       def apply(tree: Tree, resultType: Type): Aligned = tree match {
1864         case Typed(tree, _)               => apply(tree, resultType)
1865         case Apply(fn, args)              => apply(tree, fn, args, resultType)
1866         case UnApply(fn, implicits, args) => apply(tree, fn, args, resultType)
1867       }
1868     }
1869   }
1870   }
